Source Code

These source-code files were from the printout at the MIT Museum, with many thanks to Deborah Douglas, the Museum's Curator of Science and Technology, for releasing it to us. The printout was digitally photographed by Paul Fjeld. A team of volunteers transcribed the source code manually from these images or, where appropriate, modified already-transcribed but similar source Colossus 249 (Apollo 9) source code to agree with the images from the printout. Note that the page images presented online are of reduced quality, and that higher-quality images are available. Report any conversion errors or legibility problems in page images to info@sandroid.org. Notations on the program listing read, in part:

	GAP:  ASSEMBLE REVISION 055 OF AGC PROGRAM COMANCHE BY NASA 2021113-051
	10:28 APR.  1,1969
Note that the date is the date of the printout, not the date of the program revision.

Page 307 

013282,000047:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME - KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
013283,000048:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 4            DATE - 27 APRIL 1967            ASSEMBLY - PINDISK REV 17
013284,000049:                                                                                                  #  MOD BY - FILENE
013285,000050:                                                                                                  #  LOG SECTION - PINBALL GAME BUTTONS AND LIGHTS
013286,000051: 
013287,000052:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION-
013288,000053: 
013289,000054:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM PROGRAM OPERATES UNDER EXECUTIVE
013290,000055:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL AND PROCESSES INFORMATION EXCHANGED BETWEEN THE AGC AND THE
013291,000056:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTER OPERATOR.  THE INPUTS TO THE PROGRAM ARE FROM THE KEYBOARD,
013292,000057:                                                                                                  #  FROM INTERNAL PROGRAMS, AND FROM THE UPLINK.
013293,000058: 
013294,000059:                                                                                                  #  THE LANGUAGE OF COMMUNICATION WITH THE PROGRAM IS A PAIR OF WORDS
013295,000060:                                                                                                  #  KNOWN AS VERB AND NOUN.  EACH OF THESE IS REPRESENTED BY A 2 CHARACTER
013296,000061:                                                                                                  #  DECIMAL NUMBER.  THE VERB CODE INDICATES WHAT ACTION IS TO BE TAKEN, THE
013297,000062:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE INDICATES TO WHAT THIS ACTION IS APPLIED.  NOUNS USUALLY
013298,000063:                                                                                                  #  REFER TO A GROUP OF ERASABLE REGISTERS.
013299,000064: 
013300,000065:                                                                                                  #  VERBS ARE GROUPED INTO DISPLAYS, LOADS, MONITORS (DISPLAYS THAT ARE
013301,000066:                                                                                                  #  UPDATED ONCE PER SECOND), SPECIAL FUNCTIONS, AND EXTENDED VERBS (THESE
013302,000067:                                                                                                  #  ARE OUTSIDE OF THE DOMAIN OF PINBALL AND CAN BE FOUND UNDER LOG SECTION
013303,000068:                                                                                                  #  :EXTENDED VERBS:).
013304,000069: 
013305,000070:                                                                                                  #  A LIST OF VERBS AND NOUNS IS GIVEN IN LOG SECTION :ASSEMBLY AND 
013306,000071:                                                                                                  #  OPERATION INFORMATION:.
013307,000072: 
013308,000073:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCES-
013309,000074: 
013310,000075:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD:
013311,000076:                                                                                                  #  EACH DEPRESSION OF A MAIN (NAVIGATION) KEYBOARD BUTTON ACTIVATES
013312,000077:                                                                                                  #  INTERRUPT KEYRUPT1 (KEYRUPT2) AND PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO 
013313,000078:                                                                                                  #  CHANNEL 15 (CHANNEL 16).  KEYRUPT1 (KEYRUPT2) PLACES THE KEY
013314,000079:                                                                                                  #  CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY
013315,000080:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM (AT :CHARIN:), AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
013316,000081: 
013317,000082:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK:
013318,000083:                                                                                                  #  EACH WORD RECEIVED BY THE UPLINK ACTIVATES INTERRUPT UPRUPT WHICH
013319,000084:                                                                                                  #  PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE
013320,000085:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM (AT :CHARIN:) AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
013321,000086: 
013322,000087:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS:
013323,000088:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS CALL PINBALL AT :NVSUB: WITH THE DESIRED VERB/NOUN
013324,000089:                                                                                                  #  CODE IN A (LOW 7 BITS FOR NOUN, NEXT 7 BITS FOR VERB).  DETAILS
013325,000090:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBED ON REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE
013326,000091:                                                                                                  #  SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
013327,000092: 
013328,000093:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
013329,000094: 
013330,000095:                                                                                                  #        IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY EXTERNAL ACTION, THERE ARE FOUR EXITS:
013331,000096:                                                                                                  #                1)      ALL BUT (2), (3), AND (4) EXIT DIRECTLY TO ENDOFJOB.

Page 308 

013333,000098:                                                                                                  #                2)      EXTENDED VERBS GO TO THE EXTENDED VERB FAN AS PART OF THE
013334,000099:                                                                                                  #                        PINBALL EXECUTIVE JOB WITH PRIORITY 30000.  IT IS THE 
013335,000100:                                                                                                  #                        RESPONSIBILITY OF THE EXTENDED VERB CALLED TO EVENTUALLY
013336,000101:                                                                                                  #                        CHANGE PRIORITY (IF NECESSARY) AND DO AN ENDOFJOB.
013337,000102:                                                                                                  #                        ALSO PINBALL IS A NOVAC JOB.  EBANK SET FOR COMMON.
013338,000103:                                                                                                  #                3)      VERB 37.  CHANGE OF PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) CALLS :V37: IN THE
013339,000104:                                                                                                  #                        SERVICE ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO
013340,000105:                                                                                                  #                        30000.  THE NEW PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IS LEFT IN A.
013341,000106:                                                                                                  #                4)      KEY RELEASE BUTTON CALLS :PINBRNCH: IN THE DISPLAY INTERFACE
013342,000107:                                                                                                  #                        ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO 30000 IF 
013343,000108:                                                                                                  #                        THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IS OFF AND :CADRSTOR: IS NOT +0.
013344,000109: 
013345,000110:                                                                                                  #  IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY INTERNAL PROGRAMS, EXIT FROM PINBALL IS BACK
013346,000111:                                                                                                  #  TO CALLING ROUTINE.  DETAILS DESCRIBED IN REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE
013347,000112:                                                                                                  #  :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
013348,000113: 
013349,000114:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
013350,000115: 
013351,000116:                                                                                                  #        EXTERNAL INITIATION:
013352,000117:                                                                                                  #                IF SOME IMPROPER SEQUENCE OF KEY CODES IS DETECTED, THE OPERATOR
013353,000118:                                                                                                  #                ERROR LIGHT IS TURNED ON AND EXIT IS TO :ENDOFJOB:.
013354,000119: 
013355,000120:                                                                                                  #        INTERNAL PROGRAM INITIATION:
013356,000121:                                                                                                  #                IF AN ILLEGAL V/N COMBINATION IS ATTEMPTED, AN ABORT IS CAUSED
013357,000122:                                                                                                  #                (WITH OCTAL 01501).
013358,000123:                                                                                                  #                IF A SECOND ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL, AN ABORT IS
013359,000124:                                                                                                  #                CAUSED (WITH OCTAL 01206).  THERE ARE TWO WAYS TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL:
013360,000125:                                                                                                  #                1)      ENDIDLE OR DATAWAIT.
013361,000126:                                                                                                  #                2)      NVSBWAIT, PRENVBSY, OR NVSUBUSY.
013362,000127: 
013363,000128:                                                                                                  #  CONDITIONS LEADING TO THE ABOVE ARE DESCRIBED IN FORTHCOMING MIT/IL
013364,000129:                                                                                                  #  E-REPORT DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
013365,000130: 
013366,000131:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT-
013367,000132: 
013368,000133:                                                                                                  #  INFORMATION TO BE SENT TO THE DISPLAY PANEL IS LEFT IN THE :DSPTAB:
013369,000134:                                                                                                  #  BUFFERS REGISTERS (UNDER EXEC CONTROL).  :DSPOUT: (A PART OF T4RUPT)
013370,000135:                                                                                                  #  HANDLES THE PLACING OF THE :DSPTAB: INFORMATION INTO OUTPUT CHANNEL 10
013371,000136:                                                                                                  #  IN INTERRUPT.
013372,000137: 
013373,000138:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION-
013374,000139: 
013375,000140:                                                                                                  #  FRESH START AND RESTART INITIALIZE THE NECESSARY E REGISTERS FOR
013376,000141:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IN :STARTSUB:.  REGISTERS ARE:  DSPTAB BUFFER, CADRSTOR,
013377,000142:                                                                                                  #  REQRET, CLPASS, DSPLOCK, MONSAVE, MONSAVE1, VERBREG, NOUNREG, DSPLIST,
013378,000143:                                                                                                  #  DSPCOUNT, NOUT.
013379,000144:

Page 309 

013381,000146:                                                                                                  #  A COMPLETE LIST OF ALL THE ERASABLES (BOTH RESERVED AND TEMPORARIES) FOR
013382,000147:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IS GIVEN BELOW.
013383,000148: 
013384,000149:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ARE OF GENERAL INTEREST-
013385,000150: 
013386,000151:                                                                                                  #  REMARKS CARDS PRECEDE THE REFERENCED SYMBOL DEFINITION.  SEE SYMBOL
013387,000152:                                                                                                  #  TABLE TO FIND APPROPRIATE PAGE NUMBERS.
013388,000153: 
013389,000154:                                                                                                  #        NVSUB           CALLING POINT FOR INTERNAL USE OF PINBALL.
013390,000155:                                                                                                  #                        OF RELATED INTEREST     NVSBWAIT
013391,000156:                                                                                                  #                                                NVSUBUSY
013392,000157:                                                                                                  #                                                PRENVBSY
013393,000158: 
013394,000159:                                                                                                  #        ENDIDLE         ROUTINE FOR INTERNAL PROGRAMS WISHING TO GO TO SLEEP WHILE
013395,000160:                                                                                                  #                        AWAITING OPERATORS RESPONSE.
013396,000161: 
013397,000162:                                                                                                  #        DSPMM           ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY DISPLAY A DECIMAL
013398,000163:                                                                                                  #                        PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IN THE PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) LIGHTS.
013399,000164:                                                                                                  #                        (DSPMM DOES NOT DISPLAY DIRECTLY BUT ENTERS EXEC REQUEST
013400,000165:                                                                                                  #                        FOR DSPMMJB WITH PRIO 30000 AND RETURNS TO CALLER.)
013401,000166: 
013402,000167:                                                                                                  #        BLANKSUB        ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY BLANK ANY
013403,000168:                                                                                                  #                        COMBINATION OF THE DISPLAY REGISTERS R1, R2, R3.
013404,000169: 
013405,000170:                                                                                                  #        JAMTERM         ROUTINES BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY PERFORM THE
013406,000171:                                                                                                  #        JAMPROC         TERMINATE (V 34) OR PROCEED (V33) FUNCTION.
013407,000172: 
013408,000173:                                                                                                  #        MONITOR         VERBS FOR PERIODIC (1 PER SEC) DISPLAY.
013409,000174: 
013410,000175:                                                                                                  #        PLEASE PERFORM, PLEASE MARK SITUATIONS
013411,000176:                                                                                                  #                REMARKS DESCRIBING HOW AN INTERNAL ROUTINE SHOULD HANDLE
013412,000177:                                                                                                  #                THESE SITUATIONS CAN BE FOUND JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: (SEE
013413,000178:                                                                                                  #                SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
013414,000179: 
013415,000180:                                                                                                  #        THE NOUN TABLE FORMAT IS DESCRIBED ON A PAGE OF REMARKS CARDS JUST
013416,000181:                                                                                                  #        BEFORE :DSPABC: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
013417,000182: 
013418,000183:                                                                                                  #        THE NOUN TABLES THEMSELVES ARE FOUND IN LOG SECTION :PINBALL NOUN
013419,000184:                                                                                                  #        TABLES:.
013420,000185: 
013421,000186:                                                                                                  #  FOR FURTHER DETAILS ABOUT OPERATION OF THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM
013422,000187:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM, SEE THE MISSION PLAN AND/OR MIT/IL E-2129
013423,000188:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.

(Note that this doc by Green and Filene is/was available online at http://hrst.mit.edu/hrs/apollo/public/archive/1706.pdf — RSB 6/2004.)

013427,000192:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING QUOTATION IS PROVIDED THROUGH THE COURTESY OF THE AUTHORS.
013428,000193: 
013429,000194:                                                                                                  #        ::IT WILL BE PROVED TO THY FACE THAT THOU HAST MEN ABOUT THEE THAT

Page 310 

013431,000196:                                                                                                  #        USUALLY TALK OF A NOUN AND A VERB, AND SUCH ABOMINABLE WORDS AS NO
013432,000197:                                                                                                  #        CHRISTIAN EAR CAN ENDURE TO HEAR.::
013433,000198:                                                                                                  #                                        HENRY 6, ACT 2, SCENE 4
013434,000199: 
013435,000200:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ASSIGNMENTS FOR PINBALL ARE MADE ELSEWHERE
013436,000201: 
013437,000202:                                                                                                  #  RESERVED FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
013438,000203: 
013439,000204:                                                                                                  # DSPCOUNT       ERASE                   DISPLAY POSITION INDICATOR
013440,000205:                                                                                                  # DECBRNCH       ERASE                   +DEC, -DEC, OCT INDICATOR
013441,000206:                                                                                                  # VERBREG        ERASE                   VERB CODE
013442,000207:                                                                                                  # NOUNREG        ERASE                   NOUN CODE
013443,000208:                                                                                                  # XREG           ERASE                   R1 INPUT BUFFER
013444,000209:                                                                                                  # YREG           ERASE                   R2 INPUT BUFFER
013445,000210:                                                                                                  # ZREG           ERASE                   R3 INPUT BUFFER
013446,000211:                                                                                                  # XREGLP         ERASE                   LO PART OF XREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
013447,000212:                                                                                                  # YREGLP         ERASE                   LO PART OF YREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
013448,000213:                                                                                                  # HITEMOUT       =       YREGLP          TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS,MIN,SEC
013449,000214:                                                                                                  #                                                 MUST = LOTEMOUT-1.
013450,000215:                                                                                                  # ZREGLP         ERASE                   LO PART OF ZREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
013451,000216:                                                                                                  # LOTEMOUT       =       ZREGLP          TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS,MIN,SEC
013452,000217:                                                                                                  #                                                 MUST = HITEMOUT+1.
013453,000218:                                                                                                  # MODREG         ERASE                   MODE CODE
013454,000219:                                                                                                  # DSPLOCK        ERASE                   KEYBOARD/SUBROUTINE CALL INTERLOCK
013455,000220:                                                                                                  # REQRET         ERASE                   RETURN REGISTER FOR LOAD
013456,000221:                                                                                                  # LOADSTAT       ERASE                   STATUS INDICATOR FOR LOADTST
013457,000222:                                                                                                  # CLPASS         ERASE                   PASS INDICATOR CLEAR
013458,000223:                                                                                                  # NOUT           ERASE                   ACTIVITY COUNTER FOR DSPTAB
013459,000224:                                                                                                  # NOUNCADR       ERASE                   MACHINE CADR FOR NOUN
013460,000225:                                                                                                  # MONSAVE        ERASE                   N/V CODE FOR MONITOR. (= MONSAVE1-1)
013461,000226:                                                                                                  # MONSAVE1       ERASE                   NOUNCADR FOR MONITOR(MATBS) = MONSAVE+1
013462,000227:                                                                                                  # MONSAVE2       ERASE                   NVMONOPT OPTIONS
013463,000228:                                                                                                  # DSPTAB         ERASE   +13D            0-10, DISPLAY PANEL BUFFER. 11-13, C RELAYS
013464,000229:                                                                                                  # CADRSTOR       ERASE                   ENDIDLE STORAGE
013465,000230:                                                                                                  # NVQTEM         ERASE                   NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING ADDRESS
013466,000231:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = NVBNKTEM-1
013467,000232:                                                                                                  # NVBNKTEM       ERASE                   NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING BANK
013468,000233:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = NVQTEM+1
013469,000234:                                                                                                  # VERBSAVE       ERASE                   NEEDED FOR RECYCLE
013470,000235:                                                                                                  # DSPLIST        ERASE                   WAITING REG FOR DSP SYST INTERNAL USE
013471,000236:                                                                                                  # EXTVBACT       REASE                   EXTENDED VERB ACTIVITY INTERLOCK
013472,000237:                                                                                                  # DSPTEM1        ERASE   +2              BUFFER STORAGE AREA 1 (MOSTLY FOR TIME)
013473,000238:                                                                                                  # DSPTEM2        ERASE   +2              BUFFER STORAGE AREA 2 (MOSTLY FOR DEG)
013474,000239: 
013475,000240:                                                                                                  #  END OF ERASABLES RESERVED FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
013476,000241: 
013477,000242:                                                                                                  #  TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION

Page 311 

013479,000244:                                                                                                  # DSEXIT         =       INTB15+         RETURN FOR DSPIN
013480,000245:                                                                                                  # EXITEM         =       INTB15+         RETURN FOR SCALE FACTOR ROUTINE SELECT
013481,000246:                                                                                                  # BLANKRET       =       INTB15+         RETURN FOR 2BLANK
013482,000247:                                                                                                  # WRDRET         =       INTBIT15        RETURN FOR 5BLANK
013483,000248:                                                                                                  # WDRET          =       INTBIT15        RETURN FOR DSPWD
013484,000249:                                                                                                  # DECRET         =       INTBIT15        RETURN FOR PUTCOM(DEC LOAD)
013485,000250:                                                                                                  # 21/22REG       =       INTBIT15        TEMP FOR CHARIN
013486,000251:                                                                                                  # UPDATRET       =       POLISH          RETURN FOR UPDATNN, UPDATVB
013487,000252:                                                                                                  # CHAR           =       POLISH          TEMP FOR CHARIN
013488,000253:                                                                                                  # ERCNT          =       POLISH          COUNTER FOR ERROR LIGHT RESET
013489,000254:                                                                                                  # DECOUNT        =       POLISH          COUNTER FOR SCALING AND DISPLAY (DEC)
013490,000255:                                                                                                  # SGNON          =       VBUF            TEMP FOR +,- ON
013491,000256:                                                                                                  # NOUNTEM        =       VBUF            COUNTER FOR MIXNOUN FETCH
013492,000257:                                                                                                  # DISTEM         =       VBUF            COUNTER FOR OCTAL DISPLAY VERBS
013493,000258:                                                                                                  # DECTEM         =       VBUF            COUNTER FOR FETCH (DEC DISPLAY VERBS)
013494,000259:                                                                                                  # SGNOFF         =       VBUF +1         TEMP FOR +,- ON
013495,000260:                                                                                                  # NVTEMP         =       VBUF +1         TEMP FOR NVSUB
013496,000261:                                                                                                  # SFTEMP1        =       VBUF +1         STORAGE FOR SF CONST HI PART (=SFTEMP2-1)
013497,000262:                                                                                                  # HITEMIN        =       VBUF +1         TEMP FOR LOAD OF HRS,MIN,SEC
013498,000263:                                                                                                  #                                                MUST = LOTEMIN-1.
013499,000264:                                                                                                  # CODE           =       VBUF +2         FOR DSPIN
013500,000265:                                                                                                  # SFTEMP2        =       VBUF +2         STORAGE FOR SF CONST LO PART (=SFTEMP1+1)
013501,000266:                                                                                                  # LOTEMIN        =       VBUF +2         TEMP FOR LOAD OF HRS,MIN,SEC
013502,000267:                                                                                                  #                                                MUST = HITEMIN+1.
013503,000268:                                                                                                  # MIXTEMP        =       VBUF +3         FOR MIXNOUN DATA
013504,000269:                                                                                                  # SIGNRET        =       VBUF +3         RETURN FOR +,- ON
013505,000270:                                                                                                  #  ALSO MIXTEMP+1 = VBUF+4, MIXTEMP+2 = VBUF+5.
013506,000271:                                                                                                  # ENTRET         =       DOTINC          EXIT FROM ENTER
013507,000272:                                                                                                  # WDCNT          =       DOTRET          CHAR COUNTER FOR DSPWD
013508,000273:                                                                                                  # INREL          =       DOTRET          INPUT BUFFER SELECTOR (X,Y,Z, REG )
013509,000274:                                                                                                  # DSPMMTEM       =       MATINC          DSPCOUNT SAVE FOR DSPMM
013510,000275:                                                                                                  # MIXBR          =       MATINC          INDICATOR FOR MIXED OR NORMAL NOUN
013511,000276:                                                                                                  # TEM1           ERASE                   EXEC TEMP
013512,000277:                                                                                                  # DSREL          =       TEM1            REL ADDRESS FOR DSPIN
013513,000278:                                                                                                  # TEM2           ERASE                   EXEC TEMP
013514,000279:                                                                                                  # DSMAG          =       TEM2            MAGNITUDE STORE FOR DSPIN
013515,000280:                                                                                                  # IDADDTEM       =       TEM2            MIXNOUN INDIRECT ADDRESS STORAGE
013516,000281:                                                                                                  # TEM3           ERASE                   EXEC TEMP
013517,000282:                                                                                                  # COUNT          =       TEM3            FOR DSPIN

Page 312 

013519,000284:                                                                                                  # TEM4           ERASE                   EXEC TEMP
013520,000285:                                                                                                  # LSTPTR         =       TEM4            LIST POINTER FOR GRABUSY
013521,000286:                                                                                                  # RELRET         =       TEM4            RETURN FOR RELDSP
013522,000287:                                                                                                  # FREERET        =       TEM4            RETURN FOR FREEDSP
013523,000288:                                                                                                  # DSPWDRET       =       TEM4            RETURN FOR DSPSIGN
013524,000289:                                                                                                  # SEPSCRET       =       TEM4            RETURN FOR SEPSEC
013525,000290:                                                                                                  # SEPMNRET       =       TEM4            RETURN FOR SEPMIN
013526,000291:                                                                                                  # TEM5           ERASE                   EXEC TEMP
013527,000292:                                                                                                  # NOUNADD        =       TEM5            TEMP STORAGE FOR NOUN ADDRESS
013528,000293:                                                                                                  # NNADTEM        ERASE                   TEMP FOR NOUN ADDRESS TABLE ENTRY
013529,000294:                                                                                                  # NNTYPTEM       ERASE                   TEMP FOR NOUN TYPE TABLE ENTRY
013530,000295:                                                                                                  # IDAD1TEM       ERASE                   TEMP FOR INDIR ADRESS TABLE ENTRY (MIXNN)
013531,000296:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = IDAD2TEM-1, = IDAD3TEM-2.
013532,000297:                                                                                                  # IDAD2TEM       ERASE                   TEMP FOR INDIR ADRESS TABLE ENTRY (MIXNN)
013533,000298:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = IDAD1TEM+1, = IDAD3TEM-1.
013534,000299:                                                                                                  # IDAD3TEM       ERASE                   TEMP FOR INDIR ADRESS TABLE ENTRY (MIXNN)
013535,000300:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = IDAD1TEM+2, = IDAD2TEM+1.
013536,000301:                                                                                                  # RUTMXTEM       ERASE                   TEMP FOR SF ROUT TABLE ENTRY (MIXNN ONLY)
013537,000302: 
013538,000303:                                                                                                  #  END OF TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
013539,000304: 
013540,000305:                                                                                                  #  ADDITIONAL TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
013541,000306: 
013542,000307:                                                                                                  #        MPAC, THRU MPAC +6
013543,000308:                                                                                                  #        BUF, +1, +2
013544,000309:                                                                                                  #        BUF2, +1, +2
013545,000310:                                                                                                  #        MPTEMP
013546,000311:                                                                                                  #        ADDRWD
013547,000312: 
013548,000313:                                                                                                  #  END OF ADDITIONAL TEMPS FOR PINBALL EXEC ACTION
013549,000314: 
013550,000315:                                                                                                  #  RESERVED FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
013551,000316: 
013552,000317:                                                                                                  # DSPCNT         ERASE                   COUNTER FOR DSPOUT
013553,000318:                                                                                                  # UPLOCK         ERASE                   BIT1 = UPLINK INTERLOCK (ACTIVATED BY
013554,000319:                                                                                                  #                                        RECEPTION OF A BAD MESSAGE IN UPLINK)
013555,000320: 
013556,000321:                                                                                                  #  END OF ERASABLES RESERVED FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
013557,000322: 
013558,000323:                                                                                                  #  TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
013559,000324: 
013560,000325:                                                                                                  # KEYTEMP1       =       WAITEXIT        TEMP FOR KEYRUPT, UPRUPT
013561,000326:                                                                                                  # DSRUPTEM       =       WAITEXIT        TEMP FOR DSPOUT
013562,000327:                                                                                                  # KEYTEMP2       =       RUPTAGN         TEMP FOR KEYRUPT, UPRUPT
013563,000328: 
013564,000329:                                                                                                  #  END OF TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
013565,000330:

Page 313 

013567,000332:                                                                                                  #  THE INPUT CODES ASSUMED FOR THE KEYBOARD ARE,
013568,000333:                                                                                                  #        0               10000
013569,000334:                                                                                                  #        1               00001
013570,000335:                                                                                                  #        9               01001
013571,000336:                                                                                                  #        VERB            10001
013572,000337:                                                                                                  #        ERROR RES       10010
013573,000338:                                                                                                  #        KEY RLSE        11001
013574,000339:                                                                                                  #        +               11010
013575,000340:                                                                                                  #        -               11011
013576,000341:                                                                                                  #        ENTER           11100
013577,000342:                                                                                                  #        CLEAR           11110
013578,000343:                                                                                                  #        NOUN            11111
013579,000344: 
013580,000345:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT FORMAT FOR DISPLAY PANEL.  SET OUT0 TO AAAABCCCCCDDDDD.
013581,000346:                                                                                                  #  A-S   SELECT A RELAYWORD.  THIS DETERMINES WHICH PAIR OF CHARACTERS ARE
013582,000347:                                                                                                  #        ENERGIZED.
013583,000348:                                                                                                  #  B     FOR SPECIAL RELAYS SUCH AS SIGNS ETC.
013584,000349:                                                                                                  #  C-S   5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR LEFT CHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD
013585,000350:                                                                                                  #  D-S   5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR RIGHT CHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD.
013586,000351: 
013587,000352:                                                                                                  #  THE PANEL APPEARS AS FOLLOWS,
013588,000353:                                                                                                  #        MD1             MD2 (MAJOR MODE)
013589,000354:                                                                                                  #        VD1             VD2 (VERB)                      ND1             ND2 (NOUN)
013590,000355:                                                                                                  #        R1D1            R1D2            R1D3            R1D4            R1D5 (R1)
013591,000356:                                                                                                  #        R2D1            R2D2            R2D3            R2D4            R2D5 (R2)
013592,000357:                                                                                                  #        R3D1            R3D2            R3D3            R3D4            R3D5 (R3)
013593,000358: 
013594,000359:                                                                                                  #  EACH OF THESE IS GIVEN A DSPCOUNT NUMBER FOR USE WITHIN COMPUTATION ONLY
013595,000360: 
013596,000361:                                                                                                  #        MD1     25              R2D1    11              ALL ARE OCTAL
013597,000362:                                                                                                  #        MD2     24              R2D2    10
013598,000363:                                                                                                  #        VD1     23              R2D3    7
013599,000364:                                                                                                  #        VD2     22              R2D4    6
013600,000365:                                                                                                  #        ND1     21              R2D5    5
013601,000366:                                                                                                  #        ND2     20              R3D1    4
013602,000367:                                                                                                  #        R1D1    16              R3D2    3
013603,000368:                                                                                                  #        R1D2    15              R3D3    2
013604,000369:                                                                                                  #        R1D3    14              R3D4    1
013605,000370:                                                                                                  #        R1D4    13              R3D5    0
013606,000371:                                                                                                  #        R1D5    12
013607,000372: 
013608,000373:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS AN 11REGISTER TABLE (DSPTAB) FOR THE DISPLAY PANEL.
013609,000374: 
013610,000375:                                                                                                  #        DSPTAB          RELAYWD         BIT11           BITS 10-6       BITS 5-1
013611,000376:                                                                                                  #        RELADD
013612,000377:                                                                                                  #        10              1011                            MD1 (25)        MD2  (24)
013613,000378:                                                                                                  #        9               1010                            VD1 (23)        VD2  (22)
013614,000379:                                                                                                  #        8               1001                            ND1 (21)        ND2  (20)
013615,000380:                                                                                                  #        7               1000                                            R1D1 (16)

Page 314 

013617,000382:                                                                                                  #        6               0111            +R1             R1D2 (15)       R1D3 (14)
013618,000383:                                                                                                  #        5               0110            -R1             R1D4 (13)       R1D5 (12)
013619,000384:                                                                                                  #        4               0101            +R2             R2D1 (11)       R2D2 (10)
013620,000385:                                                                                                  #        3               0100            -R2             R2D3 (7)        R2D4 (6)
013621,000386:                                                                                                  #        2               0011                            R2D5 (5)        R3D1 (4)
013622,000387:                                                                                                  #        1               0010            +R3             R3D2 (3)        R3D3 (2)
013623,000388:                                                                                                  #        0               0001            -R3             R3D4 (1)        R3D5 (0)
013624,000389:                                                                                                  #                        0000        NO RELAYWORD
013625,000390: 
013626,000391:                                                                                                  #  THE 5 BIT OUTPUT RELAY CODES ARE:
013627,000392: 
013628,000393:                                                                                                  #        BLANK   00000
013629,000394:                                                                                                  #        0       10101
013630,000395:                                                                                                  #        1       00011
013631,000396:                                                                                                  #        2       11001
013632,000397:                                                                                                  #        3       11011
013633,000398:                                                                                                  #        4       01111
013634,000399:                                                                                                  #        5       11110
013635,000400:                                                                                                  #        6       11100
013636,000401:                                                                                                  #        7       10011
013637,000402:                                                                                                  #        8       11101
013638,000403:                                                                                                  #        9       11111
013639,000404: 
013640,000405:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT BITS USED BY PINBALL:
013641,000406: 
013642,000407:                                                                                                  #        KEY RELEASE LIGHT       -       BIT 5 OF CHANNEL 11
013643,000408:                                                                                                  #        VERB/NOUN FLASH         -       BIT 6 OF CHANNEL 11
013644,000409:                                                                                                  #        OPERATOR ERROR LIGHT    -       BIT 7 OF CHANNEL 11

014044,000809:                                                                                                  #  ENTER PASS 0 IS THE EXECUTE FUNCTION.  HIGHER ORDER ENTERS ARE TO LOAD
014045,000810:                                                                                                  #  DATA.  THE SIGN OF REQRET DETERMINES THE PASS, + FOR PASS 0, - FOR HIGHER
014046,000811:                                                                                                  #  PASSES.

014050,000815:                                                                                                  #  VERB = FIXED MEMORY DISPLAY, WHICH REQUIRES AN FCADR).

Page 330 

014336,001101:                                                                                                  #  NOUN TABLES
014337,001102: 
014338,001103:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE L/40, NORMAL NOUN CASE.  NOUN CODE G/E 40, MIXED NOUN CASE.
014339,001104:                                                                                                  #  FOR NORMAL CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE ECADR FOR EACH NOUN.
014340,001105:                                                                                                  #  +0 INDICATES NOUN NOT USED.  - ENTRY INDICATES MACHINE CADR (E OR F) TO
014341,001106:                                                                                                  #  BE SPECIFIED.  -1 INDICATES CHANNEL TO BE SPECIFIED.  -0 INDICATES AUGMENT
014342,001107:                                                                                                  #  OF LAST MACHINE CADR SUPPLIED.
014343,001108: 
014344,001109:                                                                                                  #  FOR MIXED CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE INDIRECT ADDRESS (IDADDREL) IN LOW
014345,001110:                                                                                                  #  10 BITS, AND THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER IN THE HIGH 5 BITS.
014346,001111: 
014347,001112:                                                                                                  #  NNTYPTAB IS A PACKED TABLE OF THE FORM MMMMMNNNNNPPPPP.
014348,001113: 
014349,001114:                                                                                                  #  FOR THE NORMAL CASE,  M-S ARE THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER.
014350,001115:                                                                                                  #                        N-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE CODE NUMBER.
014351,001116:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT CODE NUMBER.
014352,001117: 
014353,001118:                                                                                                  #  MIXED CASE,           M-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT3 CODE NUMBER    3 COMPONENT CASE
014354,001119:                                                                                                  #                        N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER
014355,001120:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
014356,001121:                                                                                                  #                        N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER    2 COMPONENT CASE
014357,001122:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
014358,001123:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER    1 COMPONENT CASE
014359,001124: 
014360,001125:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO AN INDIRECT ADDRESS TABLE (IDADDTAB) FOR MIXED CASE ONLY.
014361,001126:                                                                                                  #  EACH ENTRY CONTAINS ONE ECADR.  IDADDREL IS THE RELATIVE ADDRESS OF
014362,001127:                                                                                                  #  THE FIRST OF THESE ENTRIES.
014363,001128: 
014364,001129:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ONE ENTRY IN THIS TABLE FOR EACH COMPONENT OF A MIXED NOUN
014365,001130:                                                                                                  #  THEY ARE LISTED IN ORDER OF ASCENDING K.
014366,001131: 
014367,001132:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO A SCALE FACTOR ROUTINE NUMBER TABLE (RUTMXTAB) FOR MIXED
014368,001133:                                                                                                  #  CASE ONLY.  THERE IS ONE ENTRY PER MIXED NOUN.  THE FORM IS,
014369,001134: 
014370,001135:                                                                                                  #        QQQQQRRRRRSSSSS
014371,001136: 
014372,001137:                                                                                                  #  Q-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 3 CODE NUMBER          3 COMPONENT CASE
014373,001138:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER
014374,001139:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
014375,001140:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER          2 COMPONENT CASE
014376,001141:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
014377,001142: 
014378,001143:                                                                                                  #  IN OCTAL DISPLAY AND LOAD (OCT OR DEC) VERBS, EXCLUDE USE OF VERBS WHOSE
014379,001144:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT NUMBER IS GREATER THAN THE NUMBER OF COMPONENTS IN NOUN.
014380,001145:                                                                                                  #  (ALL MACHINE ADDRESS TO BE SPECIFIED NOUNS ARE 3 COMPONENT.)
014381,001146: 
014382,001147:                                                                                                  #  IN MULTI-COMPONENT LOAD VERBS, NO MIXING OF OCTAL AND DECIMAL DATA
014383,001148:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT WORDS IS ALLOWED.  ALARM IF VIOLATION.
014384,001149: 
014385,001150:                                                                                                  #  IN DECIMAL LOADS OF DATA, 5 NUMERICAL CHARACTERS MUST BE KEYED IN
014386,001151:                                                                                                  #  BEFORE EACH ENTER.  IF NOT, ALARM.
014387,001152:

Page 331 

014389,001154:                                                                                                  #  DISPLAY VERBS
014390,001155: 
014391,001156: 41,2353           45016        DSPABC             CS       TWO                                   
014392,001157: 41,2354           02424                           TC       COMPTEST                              
014393,001158: 41,2355           50145                           INDEX    NOUNADD                               
014394,001159: 41,2356           40002                           CS       2                                     
014395,001160: 41,2357           56132                           XCH      BUF        +2

014397,001162: 41,2361           02424                           TC       COMPTEST                              
014398,001163: 41,2362           50145                           INDEX    NOUNADD                               
014399,001164: 41,2363           40001                           CS       1                                     
014400,001165: 41,2364           56131                           XCH      BUF        +1                         
014401,001166: 41,2365           02443        DSPA               TC       DECTEST                               
014402,001167: 41,2366           02466                           TC       TSTFORDP                              
014403,001168: 41,2367           50145                           INDEX    NOUNADD                               
014404,001169: 41,2370           40000                           CS       0                                     
014405,001170: 41,2371           56130        DSPCOM1            XCH      BUF                                   
014406,001171: 41,2372           02405                           TC       DSPCOM2                               
014407,001172: 41,2373           45017        DSPB               CS       ONE

014911,001676:                                                                                                  #  INHERENTLY NOT DP SUCH AS THE CDU COUNTERS THE DISPLAY WILL BE GARBAGE.

015512,002277: 42,3517           55041                           TS       VERBSAVE                              #   IN CASE OPERATOR EXECUTED A LOWER LOAD

015514,002279: 42,3521                        ENDHMSS            EQUALS                                         
015515,002280:

Page 355 

015517,002282:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ALLOWS OTHER KEYBOARD ACTIVITY.  IT IS ENDED BY VERB TERMINATE,
015518,002283:                                                                                                  #  VERB PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, VERB RESEQUENCE,
015519,002284:                                                                                                  #  ANOTHER MONITOR, OR ANY NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES THE DSPLOCK (PROVIDED
015520,002285:                                                                                                  #  THAT THE OPERATOR HAS SOMEHOW ALLOWED THE ENDING OF A MONITOR WHICH
015521,002286:                                                                                                  #  HE HAS INITIATED THROUGH THE KEYBOARD).
015522,002287: 
015523,002288:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ACTION IS SUSPENDED, BUT NOT ENDED, BY ANY KEYBOARD ACTION,
015524,002289:                                                                                                  #  EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET.  IT BEGINS AGAIN WHEN KEY RELEASE IS PERFORMED.
015525,002290:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SAVES THE NOUN AND APPROPRIATE DISPLAY VERB IN MONSAVE.  IT SAVES
015526,002291:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR IN MONSAVE1, IF NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED.  BIT 15 OF
015527,002292:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE1 IS THE KILL MONITOR SIGNAL (KILLER BIT).  BIT 14 OF MONSAVE1
015528,002293:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES THE CURRENT MONITOR WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED (EXTERNAL
015529,002294:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR BIT).  IT IS TURNED OFF BY RELDSP AND KILMONON.
015530,002295: 
015531,002296:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE INDICATES IF MONITOR IS ON (+=ON, +0=OFF)
015532,002297:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +, MONITOR ENTERS NO REQUEST, BUT TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
015533,002298:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +0, MONITOR ENTERS REQUEST AND TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
015534,002299: 
015535,002300:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB (IF EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT IS OFF), VB=PROCEED WITHOUT DATA,
015536,002301:                                                                                                  #  VB=RESEQUENCE, AND VB=TERMINATE TURN KILL MONITOR BIT ON.
015537,002302: 
015538,002303:                                                                                                  #  IF KILLER BIT IS ON, MONREQ ENTERS NO FURTHER REQUESTS, ZEROS MONSAVE
015539,002304:                                                                                                  #  AND MONSAVE1 (TURNING OFF KILLER BIT AND EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT).
015540,002305: 
015541,002306:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR DOSENT TEST FOR MATBS SINCE NVSUB CAN HANDLE INTERNAL MATBS NOW

015670,002435: 
015671,002436:                                                                                                  #  DSPFMEM IS USED TO DISPLAY (IN OCTAL) ANY FIXED REGISTER.
015672,002437:                                                                                                  #  IT IS USED WITH NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED.  THE FCADR OF THE 
015673,002438:                                                                                                  #  DESIRED LOCATION IS THEN PUNCHED IN.  IT HANDLES F/F (FCADR 4000-7777)
015674,002439:                                                                                                  #  
015675,002440:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27, THIS IS ENOUGH.
015676,002441: 
015677,002442:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30, THE THIRD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26 (PRIO, ADRES, BBCON)
015678,002443:                                                                                                  #  MUST BE PRELOADED WITH THE DESIRED SUPERBANK BITS (BITS 5,6,7).
015679,002444:                                                                                                  #        V23N26 SHOULD BE USED.
015680,002445: 
015681,002446:                                                                                                  #  SUMMARY
015682,002447:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27,                             V27N01E(FCADR)E
015683,002448:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30,     V23N26E(SUPERBITS)E     V27N01E(FCADR)E
015684,002449: 
015685,002450: 41,3353           34333        DSPFMEM            CAF      R1D1                                  #  IF F/F, DATACALL USES BANK 02 OR 03.
015686,002451: 41,3354           54777                           TS       DSPCOUNT                              
015687,002452: 41,3355           31047                           CA       DSPTEM1    +2                         #  SUPERBANK BITS WERE PRELOADED INTO
015688,002453: 41,3356           54001                           TS       L                                     #  3RD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26.
015689,002454: 41,3357           31017                           CA       NOUNCADR                              #  ORIGINAL FCADR LOADED STILL IN NOUNCADR.
015690,002455: 41,3360           04715                           TC       SUPDACAL                              #  CALL WITH FCADR IN A, SUPERBITS IN L.
