016114,002879:                                                                                                  #  END OF LOAD.

Page 368 

016116,002881: 
016117,002882:                                                                                                  #  KEY RELEASE ROUTINE
016118,002883: 
016119,002884:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE ALWAYS TURNS OFF THE UPACT LIGHT AND ALWAYS CLEARS DSPLOCK.
016120,002885: 
016121,002886:                                                                                                  #  THE HIGHEST PRIORITY FUNCTION OF THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON IS THE
016122,002887:                                                                                                  #  UNSUSPENDING OF A SUSPENDED MONITOR WHICH WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED.
016123,002888:                                                                                                  #  THIS FUNCTION IS ACCOMPLISHED BY CLEARING DSPLOCK AND TURNING OFF
016124,002889:                                                                                                  #  THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IF BOTH DSPLIST AND CADRSTOR ARE EMPTY.
016125,002890: 
016126,002891:                                                                                                  #  IF NO SUCH MONITOR EXISTS, THEN RELDSP IS EXECUTED TO CLEAR DSPLOCK
016127,002892:                                                                                                  #  AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (FREEING THE DISPLAY SYSTEM FOR INTERNAL
016128,002893:                                                                                                  #  USE), TURN OFF THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT, AND WAKE UP ANY JOB IN DSPLIST.
016129,002894: 
016130,002895:                                                                                                  #  IN ADDITION IF THERE IS A JOB IN ENDIDLE, THEN CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED
016131,002896:                                                                                                  #  TO PINBRNCH (IN DISPLAY INTERFACE ROUTINE) TO RE-EXECUTE THE SERIES OF
016132,002897:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CALLS ETC. THAT PRECEDED THE ENDIDLE CALL STILL AWAITING RESPONSE.
016133,002898:                                                                                                  #  THIS FEATURE IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN THE OPERATOR HAS BEEN REQUESTED TO
016134,002899:                                                                                                  #  RESPOND TO SOME INTERNAL ACTION THAT USED ENDIDLE, BUT HE HAS WRITTEN
016135,002900:                                                                                                  #  OVER THE INFORMATION ON THE DISPLAY PANEL BY SOME DISPLAYS OF HIS OWN
016136,002901:                                                                                                  #  INITIATION WHICH DO NOT SERVE AS RESPONSES.  HITTING KEYRLSE WILL
016137,002902:                                                                                                  #  RE-ESTABLISH THE DISPLAYS TO THE STATE THEY WERE IN BEFORE HE OBSCURED
016138,002903:                                                                                                  #  THEM, SO THAT HE CAN SEE THE WAITING REQUEST.  THIS WORKS ONLY FOR
016139,002904:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS THAT USED ENDIDLE THROUGH MARGARETS DISPLAY
016140,002905:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES.
016141,002906: 
016142,002907: 40,3366           45015        VBRELDSP           CS       BIT3                                  
016143,002908: 40,3367           00006                           EXTEND                                         
016144,002909: 40,3370           03011                           WAND     DSALMOUT                              #  TURN OFF UPACT LITE
016145,002910: 40,3371           10115                           CCS      21/22REG                              #  OLD DSPLOCK
016146,002911: 40,3372           35002                           CAF      BIT14                                 
016147,002912: 40,3373           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (EMB)
016148,002913: 40,3374           10000                           CCS      A                                     
016149,002914: 40,3375           03404                           TC       UNSUSPEN                              #  OLD DSPLOCK AND EMB BOTH 1, UNSUSPEND.
016150,002915: 40,3376           04473        TSTLTS4            TC       RELDSP                                #  NOT UNSUSPENDING EXTERNAL MONITOR,
016151,002916: 40,3377           11042                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #        RELEASE DISPLAY SYSTEM AND
016152,002917: 40,3400           03402                           TC       +2                                    #        DO RE-ESTABLISH IF CADRSTOR IS FULL.
016153,002918: 40,3401           05217                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
016154,002919: 40,3402           04701                           TC       POSTJUMP                              
016155,002920: 40,3403           21272                           CADR     PINBRNCH                              
016156,002921: 40,3404           35021        UNSUSPEN           CAF      ZERO                                  #  EXTERNAL MONITOR IS SUSPENDED,
016157,002922: 40,3405           55012                           TS       DSPLOCK                               #        JUST UNSUSPEND IT BY CLEARING DSPLOCK.
016158,002923: 40,3406           11042                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #        TURN KEY RELEASE LIGHT OFF IF BOTH
016159,002924: 40,3407           05217                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              #        CADRSTOR AND DSPLIST ARE EMPTY.
016160,002925: 40,3410           04516                           TC       RELDSP1                               
016161,002926: 40,3411           05217                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
016162,002927: 
016163,002928: 40,3412                        ENDRELDS           EQUALS                                         
016164,002929:

Page 369 

016166,002931:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IS USED FOR SUBROUTINE CALLS FROM WITHIN COMPUTER.  IT CAN BE
016167,002932:                                                                                                  #  USED TO CALL THE COMBINATION OF ANY DISPLAY, LOAD, OR MONITOR VERB
016168,002933:                                                                                                  #  TOGETHER WITH ANY NOUN AVAILABLE TO THE KEYBOARD.
016169,002934:                                                                                                  #  PLACE 0VVVVVVVNNNNNNN INTO A.
016170,002935:                                                                                                  #  V-S ARE THE 7 BIT VERB CODE.  N-S ARE THE 7 BIT NOUN CODE.
016171,002936: 
016172,002937:                                                                                                  #  IF NVSUB IS CALLED WITH THE FOLLOWING NEGATIVE NUMBERS (RATHER THAN THE
016173,002938:                                                                                                  #  VERB-NOUN CODE) IN A, THEN THE DISPLAY IS BLANKED AS FOLLOWS-
016174,002939:                                                                                                  #  -4 FULL BLANK, -3 LEAVE MODE, -2 LEAVE MODE AND VERB, -1 BLANK R-S ONLY
016175,002940: 
016176,002941:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CAN BE USED WITH MACH CADR TO BE SPEC BY PLACING THE CADR INTO
016177,002942:                                                                                                  #  MPAC+2 BEFORE THE STANDARD NVSUB CALL.
016178,002943: 
016179,002944:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB RETURNS TO 2+ CALLING LOC AFTER PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
016180,002945:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS AVAILABLE.  THE NEW NOUN AND VERB CODES ARE DISPLAYED.
016181,002946:                                                                                                  #  IF V:S =0, THE NEW NOUN CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY (RETURN WITH NO FURTHER
016182,002947:                                                                                                  #  ACTION).  IF N-S =0, THE NEW VERB CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY (RETURN WITH NO
016183,002948:                                                                                                  #  FURTHER ACTION).
016184,002949: 
016185,002950:                                                                                                  #  IT RETURNS TO 1+ CALLING LOC WITHOUT PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
016186,002951:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS BLOCKED (NOTHING IS DISPLAYED IN THIS CASE).
016187,002952:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES TC ABORT (WITH OCT 01501) IF IT ENCOUNTERS A DISPLAY PROGRAM
016188,002953:                                                                                                  #  ALARM CONDITION BEFORE RETURN TO CALLER.
016189,002954: 
016190,002955:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS BLOCKED BY THE DEPRESSION OF ANY
016191,002956:                                                                                                  #  KEY, EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET
016192,002957:                                                                                                  #  IT IS RELEASED BY THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON, ALL EXTENDED VERBS,
016193,002958:                                                                                                  #  PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, TERMINATE, RESEQUENCE, INITIALIZE EXECUTIVE,
016194,002959:                                                                                                  #  RECALL PART OF RECALTST IF ENDIDLE WAS USED,
016195,002960:                                                                                                  #  VB = REQUEST EXECUTIVE, VB = REQUEST WAITLIST,
016196,002961:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SET UP.
016197,002962: 
016198,002963:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS ALSO BLOCKED BY THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT, WHICH
016199,002964:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES AN EXTERNALLY INITIATED MONITOR IS RUNNING (SEE MONITOR)
016200,002965: 
016201,002966:                                                                                                  #  A NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES DSPLOCK AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT ENDS OLD
016202,002967:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR.
016203,002968: 
016204,002969:                                                                                                  #  DSPLOCK IS THE INTERLOCK FOR USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM WHICH
016205,002970:                                                                                                  #  LOCKS OUT INTERNAL USE WHENEVER THERE IS EXTERNAL KEYBOARD ACTION.
016206,002971: 
016207,002972:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB SHOULD BE USED TWICE IN SUCCESSION FOR :PLEASE PERFORM: SITUATIONS
016208,002973:                                                                                                  #  (SIMILARLY FOR PLEASE MARK).  FIRST PLACE THE CODED NUMBER FOR WHAT
016209,002974:                                                                                                  #  ACTION IS DESIRED OF OPERATOR INTO THEREGISTERS REFERRED TO BY THE
016210,002975:                                                                                                  #  :CHECKLIST: NOUN.  GO TO NVSUB WITH A DISPLAY VERB AND THE :CHECKLIST:
016211,002976:                                                                                                  #  NOUN.  GO TO NVSUB AGAIN WITH THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB AND ZEROS IN THE
016212,002977:                                                                                                  #  LOW 7 BITS.  THIS :PASTES UP: THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB INTO THE VERB
016213,002978:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS.
016214,002979: 
016215,002980:                                                                                                  #  NVMONOPT IS AN ENTRY SIMILAR TO NVSUB, BUT REQUIRING AN ADDITIONAL

Page 370 

016217,002982:                                                                                                  #  PARAMETER IN L.  IT SHOULD BE USED ONLY WITH A MONITOR VERB-NOUN CODE IN
016218,002983:                                                                                                  #  A.  AFTER EACH MONITOR DISPLAY A *PLEASE* VERB WILL BE PASTED IN THE VERB
016219,002984:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS OR DATA WILL BE BLANKED (OR BOTH) ACCORDING TO THE OPTIONS
016220,002985:                                                                                                  #  SPECIFIED IN L.  IF BITS 8-14 OF L ARE OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL 
016221,002986:                                                                                                  #  BE INTERPRETED AS A VERB CODE AND PASTED IN THE VERB LIGHTS.  (THIS VERB
016222,002987:                                                                                                  #  CODE SHOULD DESIGNATE ONE OF THE *PLEASE* VERBS.)  IF BITS 1-3 OF L ARE
016223,002988:                                                                                                  #  OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL BE USED TO BLANK DATA BY BEING FED TO
016224,002989:                                                                                                  #  BLANKSUB.  IF NVMONOPT IS USED WITH A VERB OTHER THAN A MONITOR VERB,
016225,002990:                                                                                                  #  THE PARAMETER IN L HAS NO EFFECT.
016226,002991: 
016227,002992:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IN FIXED-FIXED PLACES 2+CALLING LOC INTO NVQTEM, TC NVSUBEND INTO
016228,002993:                                                                                                  #  ENTRET.  (THIS WILL RESTORE OLD CALLING BANK BITS)
016229,002994:

016340,003105:    4220                                           SETLOC   NVSUBEND   +2                         
016341,003106:    4220                                           COUNT    02/PIN                                
016342,003107:                                                                                                  #  FORCE BIT 15 OF MONSAVE1 TO 1.
016343,003108:    4220           35001        KILMONON           CAF      BIT15                                 #        THIS IS THE KILL MONITOR BIT.
016344,003109:    4221           55021                           TS       MONSAVE1                              #  TURN OFF BIT 14, THE EXTERNAL
016345,003110:                                                                                                  #        MONITOR BIT.
016346,003111:    4222           00002                           TC       Q                                     
016347,003112: 
016348,003113:                                                                                                  #  LOADSTAT      +0      INACTIVE (WAITING FOR DATA).  SET BY NVSUB
016349,003114:                                                                                                  #                +1      PROCEED NO DATA.  SET BY SPECIAL VERB
016350,003115:                                                                                                  #                -1      TERMINATE       SET BY SPECIAL VERB
016351,003116:                                                                                                  #                -0      DATA IN         SET BY END OF LOAD ROUTINE
016352,003117:                                                                                                  #                        OR RESEQUENCE   SET BY VERB 32
016353,003118: 
016354,003119:                                                                                                  #  L TC ENDIDLE (FIXED FIXED)
016355,003120:                                                                                                  #  ROUTINES THAT REQUEST LOADS THROUGH NVSUB SHOULD USE ENDIDLE WHILE
016356,003121:                                                                                                  #  WAITING FOR THE DATA TO BE LOADED.  ENDIDLE PUTS CURRENT JOB TO SLEEP.
016357,003122:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
016358,003123:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOB SLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
016359,003124:                                                                                                  #  RECALTST TESTS LOADSTAT AND WAKES JOB UP TO,
016360,003125:                                                                                                  #        L+1     FOR TERMINATE
016361,003126:                                                                                                  #        L+2     FOR PROCEED WITHOUT DATA
016362,003127:                                                                                                  #        L+3     FOR DATA IN, OR RESEQUENCE
016363,003128:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES NOTHING IF LOADSTAT INDICATES WAITING FOR DATA.

Page 373 

016365,003130: 
016366,003131:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO SLEEP
016367,003132:                                                                                                  #  IN PINBALL.  IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO ENDIDLE WHEN
016368,003133:                                                                                                  #        1)      CADRSTOR NOT= +0.  THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF ENDIDLE IS
016369,003134:                                                                                                  #                EXCEEDED.  (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
016370,003135:                                                                                                  #        2)      DSPLIST NOT= +0.  THIS INDICATES A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO
016371,003136:                                                                                                  #                NVSUBUSY.
016372,003137: 
016373,003138:    4223           22002        ENDIDLE            LXCH     Q                                     #  RETURN ADDRESS INTO L.
016374,003139:    4224           04234                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0
016375,003140:    4225           04240                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0
016376,003141:    4226           30001                           CA       L                                     #  DONT SET DSPLOCK TO 1 SO CAN USE
016377,003142:    4227           75054                           MASK     LOW10                                 #  ENDIDLE WITH NVSUB INITIATED MONITOR.
016378,003143:    4230           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  SAME STRATEGY FOR CADR AS MAKECADR.
016379,003144:    4231           55042                           TS       CADRSTOR                              
016380,003145:    4232           05175                           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
016381,003146: 
016382,003147:    4233           05217        ENDINST            TC       ENDOFJOB                              
016383,003148:

016385,003150:    4235           04243                           TC       DSPABORT                              #  RETURNS IF CADRSTOR = +0.

Page 381 

016715,003480:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
016716,003481: 
016717,003482:                                                                                                  #  USER MUST SCHEDULE CALLS TO NVSUB SO THAT THERE IS NO CONFLICT OF USE OR
016718,003483:                                                                                                  #  CONFUSION TO OPERATOR.  THE OLD GRABLOCK (INTERNAL/INTERNAL INTERLOCK)
016719,003484:                                                                                                  #  HAS BEEN REMOVED AND THE INTERNAL USER NO LONGER HAS THE PROTECTION THIS
016720,003485:                                                                                                  #  OFFERED.
016721,003486: 
016722,003487:                                                                                                  #  THERE ARE TWO WAYS A JOB CAN BE PUT TO SLEEP BY THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
016723,003488:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM.      1)      BY ENDIDLE
016724,003489:                                                                                                  #                2)      BY NVSUBUSY
016725,003490:                                                                                                  #  THE BASIC CONVENTION IS THAT ONLY ONE JOB WILL BE PERMITTED ASLEEP VIA
016726,003491:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM AT A TIME.  IF A JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
016727,003492:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP BY MEANS OF (1) OR (2) AND THERE IS ALREADY AJOB ASLEEP THAT WAS
016728,003493:                                                                                                  #  PUT TO SLEEP BY (1) OR (2), THEN AN ABORT IS CAUSED.
016729,003494: 
016730,003495:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE FOR NVSUB IS
016731,003496:                                                                                                  #                        CAF             V/N
016732,003497:                                                                                                  #        L               TC              NVSUB
016733,003498:                                                                                                  #        L+1             RETURN HERE IF OPERATOR HAS INTERVENED
016734,003499:                                                                                                  #        L+2             RETURN HERE AFTER EXECUTION
016735,003500: 
016736,003501:                                                                                                  #  A ROUTINE CALLED NVSUBUSY IS PROVIDED (USE IS OPTIONAL) TO PUT
016737,003502:                                                                                                  #  YOUR JOB TO SLEEP UNTIL THE OPERATOR RELEASES THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
016738,003503:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM.  NVSUBUSY ALSO TURNS ON THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT.
016739,003504:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
016740,003505:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOBSLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
016741,003506: 
016742,003507:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE IS
016743,003508:                                                                                                  #        CAF     WAKEFCADR
016744,003509:                                                                                                  #        TC      NVSUBUSY
016745,003510:                                                                                                  #  .
016746,003511: 
016747,003512:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN AN INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS THE OPERATOR
016748,003513:                                                                                                  #  IS USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM (BY HIS OWN INITIATION).  IT IS
016749,003514:                                                                                                  #  NOT INTENDED FOR USE WHEN ONE INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS ANOTHER INTERNAL 
016750,003515:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM.
016751,003516: 
016752,003517:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
016753,003518:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP IN PINBALL.  IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO NVSUBUSY
016754,003519:                                                                                                  #  WHEN
016755,003520: 
016756,003521:                                                                                                  #        1)      DSPLIST NOT= +0.  THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF THE DSPLIST
016757,003522:                                                                                                  #                IS EXCEEDED.
016758,003523:                                                                                                  #        2)      CADRSTOR NOT= +0.  THIS INDICATES THAT A JOB IS ALREADY USING

Page 382 

016760,003525:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE.  (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
016761,003526: 
016762,003527:    4453           44460        PRENVBSY           CS       2K+3                                  #  SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED
016763,003528:    4454           60002                           AD       Q                                     #  BANKS ONLY DESIRING THE FCADR OF (LOC
016764,003529:    4455           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  FROM WHICH THE TC PRENVBSY WAS DONE) -2
016765,003530:    4456           04701        NVSUBUSY           TC       POSTJUMP                              #  TO BE ENTERED.
016766,003531:    4457           10577                           CADR     NVSUBSY1                              
016767,003532:    4460           02003        2K+3               OCT      2003                                  
016768,003533: 
016769,003534:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBSY1 MUST BE IN BANK 27 OR LOWER, SO IT WILL PUT CALLER TO SLEEP
016770,003535:                                                                                                  #  WITH HIS PROPER SUPERBITS.
016771,003536: 
016772,003537: 04,2577                                           SETLOC   ENDSPMM    +1                         
016773,003538: 04,2577                                           COUNT    07/PIN                                
016774,003539: 
016775,003540: 04,2577           54001        NVSUBSY1           TS       L                                     
016776,003541: 04,2600           04234                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
016777,003542: 04,2601           04240                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0.
016778,003543: 04,2602           04410                           TC       RELDSPON                              
016779,003544: 04,2603           30001                           CA       L                                     
016780,003545: 04,2604           55043                           TS       DSPLIST                               
016781,003546: 04,2605           05175        ENDNVBSY           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
016782,003547: 
016783,003548:                                                                                                  #  NVSBWAIT IS A SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED BANKS ONLY. IF
016784,003549:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS NOT BUSY, IT EXECUTES V/N AND RETURNS TO L+1 (L= LOC FROM
016785,003550:                                                                                                  #  WHICH THE TC NVSBWAIT WAS DONE).  IF SYSTEM IS BUSY, IT PUTS CALLING JOB
016786,003551:                                                                                                  #  TO SLEEP WITH L-1 GOING INTO LIST FOR EVENTUAL WAKING UP WHEN SYSTEM
016787,003552:                                                                                                  #  IS NOT BUSY.
016788,003553: 
016789,003554:    4461                                           SETLOC   NVSUBUSY   +3                         
016790,003555:    4461                                           COUNT    02/PIN                                
016791,003556: 
016792,003557:    4461           22007        NVSBWAIT           LXCH     7                                     #  ZERO NVMONOPT OPTIONS
016793,003558:    4462           54123                           TS       NVTEMP                                
016794,003559:    4463           35002                           CAF      BIT14                                 
016795,003560:    4464           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT
016796,003561:    4465           61012                           AD       DSPLOCK                               
016797,003562:    4466           10000                           CCS      A                                     
016798,003563:    4467           14471                           TCF      NVSBWT1                               #  BUSY
016799,003564:    4470           14200                           TCF      NVSBCOM                               #  FREE. NVSUB WILL SAVE L+1 FOR RETURN
016800,003565:                                                                                                  #  AFTER EXECUTION.
016801,003566:    4471           24002        NVSBWT1            INCR     Q                                     #  L+2.  PRENVBSY WILL PUT L-1 INTO LIST AND
016802,003567:    4472           14453                           TCF      PRENVBSY                              #  GO TO SLEEP.
016803,003568: 
016804,003569:                                                                                                  #  RELDSP IS USED BY VBPROC, VBTERM, VBRQEXEC, VBRQWAIT, VBRELDSP, EXTENDED
016805,003570:                                                                                                  #  VERB DISPATCHER, VBRESEQ, RECALTST.
016806,003571: 
016807,003572:                                                                                                  #  RELDSP1 IS USED BY MONITOR SET UP, VBRELDSP.
016808,003573: 
016809,003574:    4473           56002        RELDSP             XCH      Q                                     #  SET DSPLOCK TO +0, TURN RELDSP LIGHT

Page 383

016952,003717:                                                                                                  #  ERROR LIGHT RESET (RSET) TURNS OFF,
016953,003718:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK ACTIVITY, AUTO, HOLD, FREE, OPERATOR ERROR,
016954,003719:                                                                                                  #  PROG ALM, TRACKER FAIL.
016955,003720: 
016956,003721:                                                                                                  #  LEAVES GIMBAL LOCK AND NO ATT ALONE.
016957,003722:                                                                                                  #  
016958,003723:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO ZEROES THE :TEST ALARM: OUT BIT, WHICH TURNS OFF STBY, RESTART.
016959,003724:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO SETS :CAUTION RESET: TO 1.
016960,003725:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO FORCES BIT 12 OF ALL DSPTAB ENTRIES TO 1.
